Now I understand the issue and the solution. The problem is in the `doFunct_RandomGen` function in `/testbed/grammar/rainerscript.c`. Currently, when the `random()` function is called with a value larger than `MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER`, it only emits a debug message using `DBGPRINTF`, but according to the PR description, it should also emit a warning to "normal" output.

The fix is to add a `LogMsg` call with `LOG_WARNING` severity in addition to the existing `DBGPRINTF` call.

Let me first create a simple test script to reproduce the issue:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_random_warning.c --file_text '#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

#define MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER RAND_MAX

// Simulate the current behavior
void current_random_behavior(long long max) {
    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
        printf("DEBUG: rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)\n", 
               max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
    }
}

// Simulate the desired behavior
void desired_random_behavior(long long max) {
    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
        printf("DEBUG: rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)\n", 
               max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
        printf("WARNING: rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)\n", 
               max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
    }
}

int main() {
    long long large_value = (long long)RAND_MAX + 1000;
    
    printf("Current behavior (only debug output):\n");
    current_random_behavior(large_value);
    
    printf("\nDesired behavior (debug + normal output):\n");
    desired_random_behavior(large_value);
    
    return 0;
}'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_random_warning.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Test script to verify the random() function warning behavior."""

import subprocess
import sys
import time
import os

def test_random_warning():
    """Test if the random() function emits warnings for unsupported values."""
    
    # Start rsyslog with test configuration
    config_file = "/testbed/test_config.conf"
    log_file = "/tmp/rsyslog_test.log"
    
    # Clean up previous log files
    if os.path.exists(log_file):
        os.remove(log_file)
    
    # Start rsyslogd with debug output
    cmd = [
        "/testbed/tools/rsyslogd",
        "-n",  # don'"'"'t fork
        "-i", "/tmp/rsyslogd.pid",
        "-f", config_file
    ]
    
    print("Starting rsyslogd...")
    process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE)
    
    # Give it time to start
    time.sleep(2)
    
    # Send a test message
    test_message = "test random function warning"
    echo_cmd = ["echo", test_message]
    nc_cmd = ["nc", "-u", "localhost", "13514"]
    
    echo_process = subprocess.Popen(echo_cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE)
    subprocess.run(nc_cmd, stdin=echo_process.stdout, capture_output=True)
    
    # Give it time to process
    time.sleep(1)
    
    # Check stderr for warning messages
    process.terminate()
    stdout, stderr = process.communicate(timeout=5)
    
    # Clean up pid file
    if os.path.exists("/tmp/rsyslogd.pid"):
        os.remove("/tmp/rsyslogd.pid")
    
    # Analyze output
    stdout_str = stdout.decode('"'"'utf-8'"'"', errors='"'"'ignore'"'"')
    stderr_str = stderr.decode('"'"'utf-8'"'"', errors='"'"'ignore'"'"')
    
    print("STDOUT:", stdout_str)
    print("=" * 50)
    print("STDERR:", stderr_str)
    
    # Check for the warning message
    debug_pattern = "desired random-number range"
    warning_pattern = "WARNING.*desired random-number range"
    
    has_debug = debug_pattern in stderr_str or debug_pattern in stdout_str
    has_warning = warning_pattern in stderr_str or warning_pattern in stdout_str
    
    print("\n" + "="*50)
    print("Test Results:")
    print(f"Has debug message about random range: {has_debug}")
    print(f"Has warning message about random range: {has_warning}")
    
    if has_debug and has_warning:
        print("✓ Test PASSED: Both debug and normal warnings are emitted!")
        return True
    elif has_debug and not has_warning:
        print("✗ Test FAILED: Only debug warning is emitted, normal warning is missing!")
        return False
    else:
        print("? Test INCONCLUSIVE: No warning messages found")
        return False

if __name__ == "__main__":
    result = test_random_warning()
    sys.exit(0 if result else 1)'

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdarg.h>

/* Mock the actual functions and structures to test the logic */
#define MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER RAND_MAX
#define LOG_WARNING 4
#define RS_RET_VAL_OUT_OF_RANGE -2012

typedef struct {
    int d_n;
    char datatype;
} svar;

typedef struct {
    void *expr[1];
} cnffunc;

typedef void* wti_t;

/* Mock DBGPRINTF */
void DBGPRINTF(const char *fmt, ...) {
    va_list args;
    va_start(args, fmt);
    printf("DEBUG: ");
    vprintf(fmt, args);
    va_end(args);
}

/* Mock LogMsg */
void LogMsg(int errno_val, int ret_code, int severity, const char *fmt, ...) {
    va_list args;
    va_start(args, fmt);
    
    if (severity == LOG_WARNING) {
        printf("WARNING: ");
    } else {
        printf("LOG[%d]: ", severity);
    }
    vprintf(fmt, args);
    va_end(args);
}

/* Mock randomNumber */
long int randomNumber() {
    return random();
}

/* Mock variable conversion functions (simplified) */
int var2Number(svar *var, int *success) {
    *success = 1;
    return var->d_n;
}

void varFreeMembers(svar *var) {
    /* Nothing to free in mock */
}

/* Mock cnfexprEval */
void cnfexprEval(void *expr, svar *result, void *usrptr, wti_t *pWti) {
    /* Set a test value */
    result->d_n = (long long)RAND_MAX + 1000; /* Value larger than MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER */
    result->datatype = '"'"'N'"'"';
}

/* The actual function we'"'"'re testing (copy from rainerscript.c with modifications) */
void doFunct_RandomGen(cnffunc *func, svar *ret, void *usrptr, wti_t *pWti) {
    int success = 0;
    svar srcVal;
    long long retVal;
    long int x;

    /* Evaluate the expression to get max value */
    cnfexprEval(func->expr[0], &srcVal, usrptr, pWti);
    long long max = var2Number(&srcVal, &success);
    
    if (!success) {
        DBGPRINTF(
            "rainerscript: random(max) didn'"'"'t get a valid '"'"'max'"'"' limit, defaulting random-number "
            "value to 0");
        retVal = 0;
        goto done;
    }
    
    if (max == 0) {
        DBGPRINTF("rainerscript: random(max) invalid, '"'"'max'"'"' is zero, , defaulting random-number value to 0");
        retVal = 0;
        goto done;
    }
    
    x = labs(randomNumber());
    
    /* This is the key part we'"'"'re testing */
    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
        DBGPRINTF(
            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)\n",
            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
        
        /* NEW: Add warning message to normal output */
        LogMsg(0, RS_RET_VAL_OUT_OF_RANGE, LOG_WARNING,
            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
    }

    retVal = (x % max);
    
done:
    ret->d.n = retVal;
    ret->datatype = '"'"'N'"'"';
    varFreeMembers(&srcVal);
}

int main() {
    cnffunc func;
    svar result;
    
    printf("Testing random() function with value larger than MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER:\n");
    printf("RAND_MAX = %d\n", RAND_MAX);
    printf("Test value = %lld\n\n", (long long)RAND_MAX + 1000);
    
    /* Call the function with a mock expression */
    doFunct_RandomGen(&func, &result, NULL, NULL);
    
    printf("\nResult: %d\n", result.d.n);
    
    return 0;
}'

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_fix.c --file_text '/* Test program to demonstrate the fix for random() function warning behavior */
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdarg.h>

#define MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER RAND_MAX
#define LOG_WARNING 4
#define RS_RET_VAL_OUT_OF_RANGE -2012

/* Mock Debug flag */
int Debug = 1;

/* Mock DBGPRINTF (debug-only output) */
#define DBGPRINTF(...)                      \
    if (Debug) {                            \
        printf("DEBUG: ");                  \
        printf(__VA_ARGS__);                \
        printf("\n");                      \
    }

/* Mock LogMsg (normal output) */
void LogMsg(int errno_val, int ret_code, int severity, const char *fmt, ...) {
    va_list args;
    va_start(args, fmt);
    
    if (severity == LOG_WARNING) {
        printf("WARNING: ");
    } else {
        printf("LOG[%d]: ", severity);
    }
    vprintf(fmt, args);
    printf("\n");
    va_end(args);
}

/* Original behavior (before fix) */
void original_random_behavior(long long max) {
    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
        /* Only debug output */
        DBGPRINTF(
            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
    }
}

/* New behavior (after fix) */
void fixed_random_behavior(long long max) {
    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
        /* Debug output */
        DBGPRINTF(
            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
        
        /* AND normal warning output (this is the fix) */
        LogMsg(0, RS_RET_VAL_OUT_OF_RANGE, LOG_WARNING,
            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
    }
}

int main() {
    long long test_value = (long long)RAND_MAX + 1000;
    
    printf("Testing random() function warning behavior fix\n");
    printf("RAND_MAX = %d\n", RAND_MAX);
    printf("Test value = %lld (larger than RAND_MAX)\n", test_value);
    
    printf("\n=== ORIGINAL BEHAVIOR (Before fix) ===\n");
    printf("With debug enabled (Debug = 1):\n");
    Debug = 1;
    original_random_behavior(test_value);
    
    printf("\nWith debug disabled (Debug = 0):\n");
    Debug = 0;
    original_random_behavior(test_value);
    
    printf("\n=== FIXED BEHAVIOR (After fix) ===\n");
    printf("With debug enabled (Debug = 1):\n");
    Debug = 1;
    fixed_random_behavior(test_value);
    
    printf("\nWith debug disabled (Debug = 0):\n");
    Debug = 0;
    fixed_random_behavior(test_value);
    
    printf("\n=== SUMMARY ===\n");
    printf("Before fix: Warning only visible with debug enabled\n");
    printf("After fix:  Warning always visible (both debug and normal output)\n");
    
    return 0;
}'

+/* Test program to demonstrate the fix for random() function warning behavior */
+#include <stdio.h>
+#include <stdlib.h>
+#include <stdarg.h>
+
+#define MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER RAND_MAX
+#define LOG_WARNING 4
+#define RS_RET_VAL_OUT_OF_RANGE -2012
+
+/* Mock Debug flag */
+int Debug = 1;
+
+/* Mock DBGPRINTF (debug-only output) */
+#define DBGPRINTF(...)                      \
+    if (Debug) {                            \
+        printf("DEBUG: ");                  \
+        printf(__VA_ARGS__);                \
+        printf("\n");                      \
+    }
+
+/* Mock LogMsg (normal output) */
+void LogMsg(int errno_val, int ret_code, int severity, const char *fmt, ...) {
+    va_list args;
+    va_start(args, fmt);
+    
+    if (severity == LOG_WARNING) {
+        printf("WARNING: ");
+    } else {
+        printf("LOG[%d]: ", severity);
+    }
+    vprintf(fmt, args);
+    printf("\n");
+    va_end(args);
+}
+
+/* Original behavior (before fix) */
+void original_random_behavior(long long max) {
+    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
+        /* Only debug output */
+        DBGPRINTF(
+            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
+            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
+            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+    }
+}
+
+/* New behavior (after fix) */
+void fixed_random_behavior(long long max) {
+    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
+        /* Debug output */
+        DBGPRINTF(
+            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
+            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
+            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+        
+        /* AND normal warning output (this is the fix) */
+        LogMsg(0, RS_RET_VAL_OUT_OF_RANGE, LOG_WARNING,
+            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
+            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
+            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+    }
+}
+
+int main() {
+    long long test_value = (long long)RAND_MAX + 1000;
+    
+    printf("Testing random() function warning behavior fix\n");
+    printf("RAND_MAX = %d\n", RAND_MAX);
+    printf("Test value = %lld (larger than RAND_MAX)\n", test_value);
+    
+    printf("\n=== ORIGINAL BEHAVIOR (Before fix) ===\n");
+    printf("With debug enabled (Debug = 1):\n");
+    Debug = 1;
+    original_random_behavior(test_value);
+    
+    printf("\nWith debug disabled (Debug = 0):\n");
+    Debug = 0;
+    original_random_behavior(test_value);
+    
+    printf("\n=== FIXED BEHAVIOR (After fix) ===\n");
+    printf("With debug enabled (Debug = 1):\n");
+    Debug = 1;
+    fixed_random_behavior(test_value);
+    
+    printf("\nWith debug disabled (Debug = 0):\n");
+    Debug = 0;
+    fixed_random_behavior(test_value);
+    
+    printf("\n=== SUMMARY ===\n");
+    printf("Before fix: Warning only visible with debug enabled\n");
+    printf("After fix:  Warning always visible (both debug and normal output)\n");
+    
+    return 0;
+}

+    }

+               max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+        printf("WARNING: rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)\n", 
+               max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+    }
+}

+    printf("\nDesired behavior (debug + normal output):\n");
+    desired_random_behavior(large_value);
+

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Test script to verify the random() function warning behavior."""
+
+import subprocess
+import sys
+import time
+import os
+
+def test_random_warning():
+    """Test if the random() function emits warnings for unsupported values."""
+    
+    # Start rsyslog with test configuration
+    config_file = "/testbed/test_config.conf"
+    log_file = "/tmp/rsyslog_test.log"
+    
+    # Clean up previous log files
+    if os.path.exists(log_file):
+        os.remove(log_file)
+    
+    # Start rsyslogd with debug output
+    cmd = [
+        "/testbed/tools/rsyslogd",
+        "-n",  # don't fork
+        "-i", "/tmp/rsyslogd.pid",
+        "-f", config_file
+    ]
+    
+    print("Starting rsyslogd...")
+    process = subprocess.Popen(cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.PIPE)
+    
+    # Give it time to start
+    time.sleep(2)
+    
+    # Send a test message
+    test_message = "test random function warning"
+    echo_cmd = ["echo", test_message]
+    nc_cmd = ["nc", "-u", "localhost", "13514"]
+    
+    echo_process = subprocess.Popen(echo_cmd, stdout=subprocess.PIPE)
+    subprocess.run(nc_cmd, stdin=echo_process.stdout, capture_output=True)
+    
+    # Give it time to process
+    time.sleep(1)
+    
+    # Check stderr for warning messages
+    process.terminate()
+    stdout, stderr = process.communicate(timeout=5)
+    
+    # Clean up pid file
+    if os.path.exists("/tmp/rsyslogd.pid"):
+        os.remove("/tmp/rsyslogd.pid")
+    
+    # Analyze output
+    stdout_str = stdout.decode('utf-8', errors='ignore')
+    stderr_str = stderr.decode('utf-8', errors='ignore')
+    
+    print("STDOUT:", stdout_str)
+    print("=" * 50)
+    print("STDERR:", stderr_str)
+    
+    # Check for the warning message
+    debug_pattern = "desired random-number range"
+    warning_pattern = "WARNING.*desired random-number range"
+    
+    has_debug = debug_pattern in stderr_str or debug_pattern in stdout_str
+    has_warning = warning_pattern in stderr_str or warning_pattern in stdout_str
+    
+    print("\n" + "="*50)
+    print("Test Results:")
+    print(f"Has debug message about random range: {has_debug}")
+    print(f"Has warning message about random range: {has_warning}")
+    
+    if has_debug and has_warning:
+        print("✓ Test PASSED: Both debug and normal warnings are emitted!")
+        return True
+    elif has_debug and not has_warning:
+        print("✗ Test FAILED: Only debug warning is emitted, normal warning is missing!")
+        return False
+    else:
+        print("? Test INCONCLUSIVE: No warning messages found")
+        return False
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    result = test_random_warning()
+    sys.exit(0 if result else 1)

+/* Test program to verify random() function warning behavior */
+#include <stdio.h>
+#include <stdlib.h>
+#include <stdarg.h>
+
+/* Mock the actual functions and structures to test the logic */
+#define MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER RAND_MAX
+#define LOG_WARNING 4
+#define RS_RET_VAL_OUT_OF_RANGE -2012
+
+/* Mock Debug flag */
+int Debug = 1;
+
+/* Mock DBGPRINTF replaced with actual rsyslog logic */
+#define DBGPRINTF(...)                      \
+    if (Debug) {                            \
+        printf("DEBUG: ");                  \
+        printf(__VA_ARGS__);                \
+        printf("\n");                      \
+    }
+
+/* Mock LogMsg */
+void LogMsg(int errno_val, int ret_code, int severity, const char *fmt, ...) {
+    va_list args;
+    va_start(args, fmt);
+    
+    if (severity == LOG_WARNING) {
+        printf("WARNING: ");
+    } else {
+        printf("LOG[%d]: ", severity);
+    }
+    vprintf(fmt, args);
+    printf("\n");
+    va_end(args);
+}
+
+/* Simplified test function without complex structures */
+void test_random_behavior(long long max) {
+    /* Simulate the original behavior */
+    printf("=== ORIGINAL BEHAVIOR (before fix) ===\n");
+    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
+        DBGPRINTF(
+            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
+            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
+            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+    }
+    
+    printf("\n=== NEW BEHAVIOR (after fix) ===\n");
+    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
+        DBGPRINTF(
+            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
+            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
+            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+        LogMsg(0, RS_RET_VAL_OUT_OF_RANGE, LOG_WARNING,
+            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
+            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
+            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+    }
+}
+
+/* The actual function we're testing (copy from rainerscript.c with modifications) */
+void doFunct_RandomGen(cnffunc *func, svar *ret, void *usrptr, wti_t *pWti) {
+    int success = 0;
+    svar srcVal;
+    long long retVal;
+    long int x;
+
+    /* Evaluate the expression to get max value */
+    cnfexprEval(func->expr[0], &srcVal, usrptr, pWti);
+    long long max = var2Number(&srcVal, &success);
+    
+    if (!success) {
+        DBGPRINTF(
+            "rainerscript: random(max) didn't get a valid 'max' limit, defaulting random-number "
+            "value to 0");
+        retVal = 0;
+        goto done;
+    }
+    
+    if (max == 0) {
+        DBGPRINTF("rainerscript: random(max) invalid, 'max' is zero, , defaulting random-number value to 0");
+        retVal = 0;
+        goto done;
+    }
+    
+    x = labs(randomNumber());
+    
+    /* This is the key part we're testing */
+    if (max > MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER) {
+        DBGPRINTF(
+            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
+            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)\n",
+            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+        
+        /* NEW: Add warning message to normal output */
+        LogMsg(0, RS_RET_VAL_OUT_OF_RANGE, LOG_WARNING,
+            "rainerscript: desired random-number range [0 - %lld] "
+            "is wider than supported limit of [0 - %d)",
+            max, MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER);
+    }
+
+    retVal = (x % max);
+    
+done:
+    ret->d.n = retVal;
+    ret->datatype = 'N';
+    varFreeMembers(&srcVal);
+}
+
+int main() {
+    cnffunc func;
+    svar result;
+    
+    printf("Testing random() function with value larger than MAX_RANDOM_NUMBER:\n");
+    printf("RAND_MAX = %d\n", RAND_MAX);
+    printf("Test value = %lld\n\n", (long long)RAND_MAX + 1000);
+    
+    /* Call the function with a mock expression */
+    doFunct_RandomGen(&func, &result, NULL, NULL);
+    
+    printf("\nResult: %d\n", result.d.n);
+    
+    /* Test with Debug enabled */
+    Debug = 1;
+    printf("Testing with Debug = 1\n");
+    test_random_behavior(test_value);
+    
+    printf("\n");
+    
+    /* Test with Debug disabled */
+    Debug = 0;
+    printf("Testing with Debug = 0\n");
+    test_random_behavior(test_value);
+    
+    return 0;
+}
